[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the shadowsocks codebase [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing with AddressSanitizer. The issue occurs in the `json_parse_ex` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at line [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m of `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m`, where a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation attempts to access memory beyond the allocated buffer boundary. The [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability is triggered when processing JSON input through the `json_fuzz` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a heap-buffer-overflow error detected by AddressSanitizer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing operations. Specifically:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Type**: This is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability with a [0m[32m"READ [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mof size 1"[0m[39m operation. AddressSanitizer has assigned it a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a [0m[32m"1-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow"[0m[39m.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location of the Issue**: The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b7[0m[39m`, which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis located exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated region [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5020000000b7[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This indicates that the code is attempting to read one byte [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately past the end of a legitimately allocated buffer.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack Analysis**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution path:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `[0m[35m/src/[0m[95mjson_fuzz.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m12[0m[39m` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreceives input[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This calls `json_parse` at `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m958[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Which in turn calls `json_parse_ex` at `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m310[0m[39m`, where [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe actual overflow occurs at column [0m[1;36m45[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Memory Allocation**: The problematic [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer was allocated through the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing chain:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `malloc` called from the memory allocator[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `operator [0m[1;35mnew[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `fuzzer::RunOneTest` during the fuzzer's test execution[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Observations**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer size is only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes, which is relatively small and suggests either a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvery short input string or a substring/token being processed[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow happens at the exact boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating the code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlikely lacks proper bounds checking or has an off-by-one error[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code analysis, I've identified a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability** in the JSON parser's Unicode escape sequence[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling at line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m of `src/json.c`. This is an off-by-one error in bounds [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs in the `json_parse_ex` function when parsing Unicode [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in JSON strings:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Current State**: When the parser encounters `\u`, `state.ptr` points to the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'u'[0m[39m character[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Faulty Check**: Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m checks `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` before reading [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer Overread**: Lines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m310[0m[39m use `*++ state.ptr` four times, which:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pre-increments the pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmoves to next position[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Then dereferences it [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreads the value[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reads at positions: ptr+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, ptr+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, ptr+[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, ptr+[0m[1;36m4[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **The Bug**: When `end - state.ptr == [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` exactly:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The check `[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` evaluates to FALSE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcheck passes[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fourth increment moves to ptr+[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, which equals `end` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout of bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Attempts to read [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte past the allocated buffer boundary[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Concrete Example[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTest case `[0m[32m":\ucfe"[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes total[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Position [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m: `"`, `:`, `\`, `u`, `c`, `f`, `e`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When at position [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'u'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `end - state.ptr = [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check `[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` is FALSE → continues[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reads positions [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m successfully, but attempts to read position [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat `end`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ **overflow**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Other Similar Checks Are Correct[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39msurrogate pairs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` after already advancing past the first[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape - correctly positioned[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Lines [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparsing [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Check after consuming [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe first character of the keyword - correct pattern[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `src/json.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change**: Modify the bounds check from `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m306[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Rationale[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Correct Bounds Logic**: To safely read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters using `*++ state.ptr` four[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimes starting from the current position, we need:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current position [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m[32m'u'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Four hex digits to read: [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Total required: [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes from `state.ptr` to `end`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistency**: This aligns with the pattern at line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, which checks `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough from a different starting position[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Single character modification [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with no side [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meffects[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Complete Fix**: This addresses the exact root cause without affecting other [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The change only affects the boundary condition, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall other parsing logic remains intact[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid Unicode escapes with [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits will still parse correctly[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid escapes with fewer than [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits will now be properly rejected [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of causing buffer overreads[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The two-pass parsing mechanism remains unchanged[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m encoding logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m340[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m379[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unaffected[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Addresses Only the Vulnerability**: No modifications to:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_fuzz.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test infrastructure[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - String handling macros[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other escape sequence handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m299[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m303[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m320[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m338[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistent Error Handling**: The existing error reporting mechanism [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m312[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandles the boundary violation appropriately[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Verification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith the fix applied:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Vulnerable input** `[0m[32m":\ucfe"[0m[39m`: At position [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, `[0m[1;36m7[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m` → TRUE → error [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraised ✓[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Valid input** `[0m[32m":\ucfed"[0m[39m`: At position [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, `[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m` → FALSE → continues [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing ✓[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Minimal valid** `[0m[32m"\u0000"[0m[39m`: At position [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, `[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m` → FALSE → parses [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly ✓[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected, as this change only makes the bounds [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck more restrictive in an edge case that previously caused undefined behavior.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
